			owner = {
				OR = {
					c:PRU ?= this
					c:GER ?= this
					c:NGF ?= this
				}
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						c:ZAN ?= this
						any_primary_culture = { cu:bedouin = this }
						NOT = { any_primary_culture = { cu:swahili = this } }
					}
					any_primary_culture = {
						OR = {
							cu:polish = this
							cu:lithuanian = this
							cu:hungarian = this
						}
					}
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:romanian
					was_formed_from = AUS
					c:TUR ?= this
					c:RUS ?= this
					c:PAP ?= this
					c:GBR ?= this
					c:KOR ?= this
					c:CHI ?= this
					c:JAP ?= this
					c:AUS ?= this
					OR = {
						c:BIC ?= this
						any_primary_culture = {
							has_discrimination_trait_group = heritage_group_south_asian
						}
					}
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:hawaiian
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:australian
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:norwegian
					OR = {
						AND = {
							c:USA ?= this
							NOT = { exists = c:CSA }
						}
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:dixie
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = ig_junkers_RU_IG_TP

			is_interest_group_type = ig_devout
			owner = {
				AND = {
					country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
					OR = {
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:yankee
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:dixie
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:afro_american
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:cherokee
					}
					NOT = { c:BIC ?= this }
				}
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:ibadi
						NOT = { c:ZAN ?= this }
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:mahayana
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:japanese
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:shinto
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:japanese
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:hawaiian
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
						OR = {
							country_has_primary_culture = cu:maori
							country_has_primary_culture = cu:australian
							country_has_primary_culture = cu:anglo_canadian
							country_has_primary_culture = cu:british
							country_has_primary_culture = cu:irish
							c:NRU ?= this
						}
					}
					country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
					OR = {
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:russian
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:byelorussian
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:ukrainian
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:danish
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:norwegian
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:swedish
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:finnish
					}
					AND = {
						country_has_state_religion = rel:mahayana
						OR = {
							country_has_primary_culture = cu:korean
							any_primary_culture = {
								has_discrimination_trait = heritage_han
							}
						}
					}
					c:PAP ?= this
					c:TPG ?= this
					country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
					country_has_state_religion = rel:sunni
					country_has_state_religion = rel:shiite
					country_has_state_religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
					country_has_state_religion = rel:hindu
					country_has_state_religion = rel:gelugpa
					country_has_state_religion = rel:theravada
					country_has_state_religion = rel:mahayana
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = ig_evangelicals_RU_IG_PP
	}

### CUSTOM FUNCTIONS | КАСТОМНЫЕ ФУНКЦИИ ###
getNameIBEorSPA_RU_VP = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no
	text = {
		trigger = {
			c:SPA ?= this
		}
		localization_key = rootgetname_RU_VP
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			c:IBE ?= this
		}
		localization_key = IBE_var_RU_VP
	}
}

getSpainName_RU_RP = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no
	text = {
		trigger = {
			c:SPA ?= this
		}
		localization_key = rootgetname_RU_RP
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			c:IBE ?= this
		}
		localization_key = SPA_var_RU_RP
	}
}
